defined_text = {
	name = get_player_3_hand_icons
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_hand_icons
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = get_player_3_card_at_1
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = no_card
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_1 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_1_full
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_2 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_1_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = get_player_3_card_at_2
	random = no

		localisation_key = no_card

		}

		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_2_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

		trigger = { always = yes }
	}

defined_text = {
	name = get_player_3_card_at_5
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = no_card
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_5 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_5_full
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_6 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_5_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = get_player_3_card_at_10
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = no_card
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_10 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_10_full
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_11 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_10_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

		trigger = { always = yes }
	}

		}
	}

		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_14_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = no_card
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_15 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_15_full
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_16 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_15_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = get_player_3_card_at_16
	random = no
	text = {
		localisation_key = no_card
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_16 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_16_full
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { blackjack_player_3_hand_17 = 1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = player_3_card_at_16_part
		trigger = { always = yes }
	}
}
